The\n * option is European, exercised only on the exercise date.\n * <p>\n * For example, a call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange is the option to perform a foreign exchange on the expiry\n * date, where USD 1.41 is paid to receive EUR 1.00.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class FxVanillaOption\n    implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxVanillaOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * Whether the option is long or short.\n   * <p>\n   * At expiry, the long party will have the option to enter in this transaction; the short party will, at the option of\n   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LongShort longShort;\n  /**\n   * The expiry date of the option.\n   * <p>\n   * The option is European, and can only be exercised on the expiry date.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LocalDate expiryDate;\n  /**\n   * @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final FxSingle underlying;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxVanillaOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, and underlying payment date.\n   * <p>\n   * No payment date adjustments apply.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate) {\n\n    return of(longShort, expiry, currencyPair, putCall, strike, baseNotional, paymentDate, null);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxVanillaOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, underlying payment date, and payment date adjustment.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @ImmutableValidator\n  private void validate() {\n    inOrderOrEqual(expiryDate, underlying.getPaymentDate(), \"expiryDate\", \"underlying.paymentDate\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  /**\n   * Gets currency pair of the base currency and counter currency.\n   * <p>\n   * This currency pair is conventional, thus indifferent to the direction of FX.\n   *\n   * @return the currency pair\n   */\n  @Override\n  public CurrencyPair getCurrencyPair() {\n    return underlying.getCurrencyPair();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the expiry date-time.\n   * <p>\n   * The option expires at this date and time.\n   * <p>\n   * The result is returned by combining the expiry date, time and time-zone.\n   *\n   * @return the expiry date and time\n   */\n  @Override\n  public ZonedDateTime getExpiry() {\n    return expiryDate.atTime(expiryTime).atZone(expiryZone);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public ResolvedFxVanillaOption resolve(ReferenceData refData) {\n    return specified future time\n * only when barrier event occurs (knock-in option) or does not occur (knock-out option).\n * <p>\n * Depending on the barrier defined in {@link Barrier}, the options are classified into four types: up-and-in,\n * down-and-in, up-and-out and down-and-out.\n * <p>\n * For example, an up-and-out call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange with barrier of 1.5 is the option to\n * perform a foreign exchange on the expiry date, where USD 1.41 is paid to receive EUR 1.00, only when EUR/USD rate does\n * not exceed 1.5 during the barrier event observation period.\n * <p>\n * In case of the occurrence (non-occurrence for knock-in options) of the barrier event, the option becomes worthless,\n * or alternatively, a rebate is made.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class FxSingleBarrierOption\n    implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * The underlying FX European option.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final FxEuropeanOption underlyingOption;\n  /**\n   * The barrier description.\n   * <p>\n   * The barrier level stored in this field must be represented based on the direction of the currency pair in the\n   * underlying FX transaction.\n   * <p>\n   * For example, if the underlying option is an option on EUR/GBP, the barrier should be a certain level of EUR/GBP rate.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final Barrier barrier;\n  /**\n   * For a 'out' option, the amount is paid when the barrier is reached;\n   * for a 'in' option, the amount is paid at expiry if the barrier is not reached.\n   * <p>\n   * This is the notional amount represented in one of the currency pair.\n   * The amount should be positive.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(get = \"optional\")\n  private final CurrencyAmount rebate;\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","numLines":80,"startLine":1,"totalLines":517}}}
